 fasebuk kii company whatsapp ne phek news or afvaahon se nipatane ke liye ek bada kadam uthaaya he
 Although the company started it already
 darasal massej forward karne par watsap ne pichley saal limit lagaaya tha
 One person could forward a whatsapp message in 20 individual or group at a time
 lekin ab company ne isaki limit kam kar di he
 Now a user can forward only five messages
 dilachasp ye he ki 5 yujar ko maisaj forward karne ke liye taiyaar kiya gaya apadet bharat main pichley saal july main hi aa chukaa tha
 But now the company has announced to make this feature global
 yani ab duniya bhar ke watsap yugers bhi ek baar main sirf paanch logon ko hi watsap massej forward kar paaenge
 According to a Reuters report, whatsapp's Policy and Communication Vice President Victoria Grand has said, 'from today the limit of whatsapp message forwarding is being reduced to 5 for whatsapp users around the world'
 company ke adhikariyon ne kaha he ki watsap massej forward ko limit karke galat jaankaree or afvaahon se ladaa ja saktaa he
 Significantly, to prevent fake news and rumors, whatsapp has started giving labels in forwarded messages
 iske alaava bharat ke akhbaar or tivi par vigyaapan ke jariye logon ko phek news or afvaahon ko rokane ko kaha ja rahaa he
 Apart from fake news and rumors, whatsapp is also in the news about child pornography
 company ne isi kram main 1 lakh 30 hajaar acounts delit kiye hai
 For this, the company has taken the help of Artificial Intelligence tool and the accounts have been deleted on suspicion of illegal activity
 israeli enjio kii ek report main kaha gaya tha ki bharat main bhi aise saikadon group active he jo child pornography ke naam par hai or inamen aapattijanak videos share kiye jate hai
 According to whatsapp, the company maintains a zero tolerance policy on such matters and the most advanced technology is being used to deal with it
 ye technolji profile photose or discripshan scan karti he auki child pornography se jude hone ke shaq par un acounts ko bain kar diya jaataa he
 Since whatsapp's chats are encrypted end to end and in such a situation no one other than the sender and receiver can read the chat
 isliye company chat ke contant ko nahin dekh sakati he
 The company has designed Artificial Intelligence based tool to remove such accounts
 purv bhartiya nausainik kulbhushan jadhav ko pakistan main maut kii sajaa sunaae jane ke baad desh main aakrosh kii lahar he
 Pakistan has accused Kulbhushan Jadhav of espionage in Pakistan as an agent of RAW
 duniyabar main saikadon varshon se jasusi hoti rahi he
 In the ancient times, king-maharaja used to spy on his enemies
 nae jamaane main har desh ne jasusi ke liye khufia agenciyon kii sthapana kii, jinka kaam sarkaar, raajnneetik dal yaa mahatvapurn shaks kii jasusi karnaa hota he
 Let's know about the top 5 intelligence agencies of the world
 
 
 1- bharat kaa rawbarawa kii khufia agency ro yani research and analysis wing ko duniya kii taqatvar khufia agency mana gaya he
 It was founded in 1968
 iskaa mukhyalay dilli main he
 The specialty of this agency is that it is not accountable to anyone but the Prime Minister of India
 ro videshi maamalon, aparaadhiyon, aatankiyon ke bare main puri jaankaree rakhti he
 At the same time, the Intelligence Bureau (IB) also works for the security of the country
 donon agenciyon ne milakar kai bade aatanki hamalon ko naakaam kiya he
 2- Pakistan's ISI Pakistan's intelligence agency ISI, ie Inter Services Intelligence, is considered the world's number one intelligence agency
 isaki sthapana saal 1948 main hui thi
 It is headquartered in Shahrah a Sohrawardy, Islamabad
 isaki neenv australian mul ke british army officer major general aar
 Cathom, who was then chief of the Pakistani Army Staff
 desh kii suraksha ke naam par iesai par aae din aatankwaad ko badhaava dene ke aarope lagate hai
 He is believed to have a hand in many terrorist attacks
 3- america kii ciaamerika kii khufia agency siie yani central intelegence agency kii sthapana saal 1947 main hui thi
 It is headquartered in Virginia, near Washington
 siie ko america hi nahin duniya main sabase zyada sakasham or taqatvar maani jaati he
 In addition to the CIA, the three agencies in the US are the NSA, the DIA, and the FBI
 siie kaa kaam sibar krime, aatankwaad rokane samet videshon se soochna ekatrit karnaa he
 In 2013, the Washington Post named the CIA the highest-budget intelligence agency
 4- israel kaa mossadijaraila kii khufia agency mosaad ko duniya kii sabase behtareen or khatarnaak khufia agenciyon main gina jaataa he
 It was established in the year 1949
 iskaa nideshak sidhe pradhanmantri ko report karata he
 Mossad means death
 kaha jaataa he ki ek baar jo mosaad kii nigaah main chadh gaya, uskaa bachanaa mushkil he
 The dreaded agents of Mossad have the power to trace him from any corner of the world
 mosaad kii pahunch har us jagah tak he, jahaan isroyal yaa uske nagarikon ke khilaaf koi bhi sajeesh rachi ja rahi ho
 5- China's MSS is China's largest intelligence agency MSS, ie Ministry of State Security
 isaki sthapana 1983 main hui thi
 It is headquartered in Beijing
 isaki kaam bhi baaki deshon kikhufia agencyki tarah he, lekin yah desh ko rajnatik rup se surakshit rakhane ke liye kaam karti he

 desh main ek varg dwaara yah baat kahi jaati rahi he ki sardaar patel desh ke pehle pradhanmantri hote to aisa hota, vaisaa hota
 It is a different matter that even if Sardar Patel became PM, he would have been able to live only for three years after independence, because he died in 1950
 lekin kya patel ke liye kabhi piem banane ke halaat the? kya ve piem ban sakate the? is sawaal kaa ek saaf jawaab to yah he ki jab tak nehru congress main the, tab tak to aisa nahin ho paata
 Let's know the reason for what is
 kaise mila bharat ko pehla pradhanmantridwitiya vishwa yuddh ke baad british hukumat kaaphi kamjor ho gai thi
 In 1946, the British Government made a Cabinet Mission Plan, under which some British officers got the responsibility to talk to Indian leaders for the independence of India
 faisla ye hua ki bharat main ek antarim sarkaar banegi
 The Viceroy's Executive Council was to be formed as an interim government
 angrej vysarai ko iskaa adhyaksh hona tha, jabaki congress party ke adhyaksh ko is council kaa vaais president bananaa tha
 Later, after independence, this Vice President was almost certain to become Prime Minister
 us samay moulana abul kalam aaazaad congress party ke adhyaksh the
 He had remained in this post since 1940 due to many big leaders being in jail
 moulana aaazaad is vakt par pad nahin chhodana chaahate the, lekin mahatma gandhi ke dabaav main ve pad chhodane ke liye raji hue or phir iske baad congress ke agle adhyaksh kii talash shuru hui jo bharat ke pehle pradhanmantri bhi banate
 Also read: Did Sardar Patel consider RSS responsible for Mahatma Gandhi's assassination? Congress Working Committee meeting was convened in April 1946 to decide this
 is baithak main mahatma gandhi, nehru, sardaar patel, acharya kriplani, rajendra prasad, khan abdul gaffaar khan sahit kai bade congressi netaa shaamil the
 Mahatma Gandhi wanted Pandit Nehru to be the president of the Congress
 vah ek lokapriy jan netaa the, lekin congress kii prantiy samitiyon main unka samarthan karne vaale kam log the
 12 out of 15 provincial committees supported the name of Sardar Patel
 In the meeting, then General Secretary of the party, JB Kripalani said, 'bapu is tradition that the election of the President of Congress is done by the Provincial Congress Committees, any Provincial Congress Committee has made Jawahar Lal Nehru's name has not been proposed for the post of president

 Sushila said that there was about four-five feet of water in the tank and she stood in it all day and kept calling for help but no one heard her voice
 usne bataaya ki raat tak jaise taise farshi ko khiskaaya or ungliyaan baahar nikaalkar awaajen lagaayee tab logon ne use baahar nikaala

 While writing on micro-blogging website Twitter about the thick beard of the Maulanas (religious leaders) of Saudi Arabia, Soad al-shaimri did not think that his thoughts could get him jailed, but that is what happened
 
 
 mahilaon ke adhikaron kii baat karne vaali talakshuda 42-varshiya soad al-shaimari ne dadhi rakhane vaale kai purushon kii tasviren post kin, jinamein ek paramparawaadi yahudee, ek hippie, ek communist, ek turki khaliph, ek sikh tathaa ek muslim tha
 
 
 Soad al-shaymari wrote with these pictures that just by keeping a beard does not make a person holy or Muslim
 
 
 usne is ore bhi dhyaan dilaayaa ki paigambar mohammad ke samay main islam ke sabase kattar aalochakon main se ek kii dadhi paigambar se bhi lambii thi
 
 
 Making such outlandish remarks is not new to Soad al-shaymari, the mother of six children who graduated in Islamic law
 
 
 ek bade kabeeley ke dharmaparayan parivaar main janmi soad bachapan main bhale hi bheden charaati raheen, lekin ab vah mahila adhikaron kii maang karne vaali udaaravaadi kaaryakarta hai, or aksar islam ko lekar die apane tarkon se saudi arab kii shaktishaalee dharmik satta ko chunauti detii rahati hai
 
 
 Soad of his ideas has to pay a price as well
 
 
 vah 'janabhaawanaaon ko bhadakaane ke liye' bina kisi aupchaarik aarope ke teen maheene jail main bitaa chuki hai
 
 
 The government has banned their foreign visits
 
 
 unke online forum 'free saudi librals network' ke sah-sansthaapak or blogar rafe badavi 10 saal kaid kii sazaa kaat rahe hai, or unhen saarvajanik rup se 50 kode bhi lagaae gaye the
 
 
 Soad's father has publicly refused to accept her daughter
 
 
 lekin itnaa sab bhi soad al-shaimari kii awaz ko dabaane ke liye kaaphi nahin tha
 
 
 Soad al-shaymari says, "I have some rights, which i think are not against my religion
 
 
 main un adhikaron ko maangana chaahati hum, or chaahati hum ki jo log faisle karte hai, ve meri baat sunen or phir kuch karen
 
 
 " arab deshon main mahila islamic scollar or kaaryakarta khuda ke saamne purushon or mahilaon ko ek samaan darja dene vaale sharia kanoonon kii nae sire se vyakhya karne kii lambey arase se maang karti aa rahi hai
 
 
 Soad al-shamari is considered to be one of the most vocal and active religious and women's rights advocates in Saudi Arabia
 
 
 soad ke mitra tathaa saathi kaaryakarta sahar nasif kaa kahana he, "unhen (soad al-shaimari ko) apni kahi baat par puraa bharosa hota he, or vah katai hichakati nahin hai
 
 
 He comes from an Arab background, a desert environment
 
 
 unhen apni prishthbhumi par fakhr he, lekin isi prishthbhumi kii vajah se vah sabhi ke saath kuch rukhi ho jaati hai, or apane vichaar vyakt karte hue bahut rukhi
 
 
 " hil praant main ek kisaan ke 12 bacchon main se sabase badi santan ke rup main pali-badi soad al-shaimari bhedon kaa dhyaan rakhti thim
 
 
 She was not only religious, but lived as a 'salafi' (a Muslim who accepts and accepts literal interpretations of Islamic laws as they are)
 
 
 uniwarsity of hil se islamic kanoon main snaatak kii degree lene ke baad soad al-shaimari public skool teacher ban gayi
 
 
 At the age of 17, Soad married a man twice as old as his own clan, and then had a daughter - Yara
 
 
 20 saal kii umr main soad kaa talaak ho gaya, or unhone phir shaadi kar lee
 
 
 Soad's second marriage to the same chief judge of Haile, who had seen his divorce case
 
 
 iske baad adhikaron ke liye soad al-shaimari kii jang us din shuru hui, jis din unki beti ko unase chin liya gaya
 
 
 As Yara turned seven, her custody was handed over to Soad's first husband
 
 
 chunki soad duusari shaadi kar chuki thim, so, adaalat ne faisla diya ki kisi duusare purush ke saath rahane kii jagah bacchee ko uske pita ke saath rahanaa chahie
 
 
 Soad al-shaymari says, "when they took him (yara) from me, and said, 'this is the will of Allah' and 'this is Islam', right then the spark of rebellion ignited in me
 
 
 aisa ho hi nahin saktaa ki duniya main aisa koi khuda he, jo is ninsaphi or takalif ko sirf isliye bardaasht kar legaa, kyonki main ek aurat hum
 
 
 " vah apni beti ko dekh bhi nahin sakati thi, so, aath saal tak vah apane mata-pita, apane samudaay ke alaava apane va apni beti yaara ke bich aane vaale har shaks se ladati rahi
 
 
 Talking handsomely with a proud face, Soad al-shaimri says, "I was getting mad, but in front of my parents, in front of my judge husband, and in front of the people in our community around them, Because of my name and my place in the community, i was expected to sit quietly watching everything
 
 
 " Soad al-shaymari had five children from his second marriage, but he was divorced soon thereafter
 
 
 jab yaara ke pita biimaar ho gaye, or uski daadi guzar gayi, tab 16 saal kii ho chuki yaara ke pita ne aakhirkaar use uski maa ke saath rahane kii ijazat de di, or soad al-shaimari apane sabhi chah bacchon ke saath zyaada udaar kahe jane vaale shahar jedda aa bases
 
 
 Soad used his knowledge of Sharia law as a legal adviser to women in need
 
 
 kabhi-kabhi unki di salahen dharmanishth kam hoti thim, kapat or nirlajjataa se bhari zyaada
 
 
 Once, he advised a friend to find out which judge is looking into his case, then put on some make-up, and cry in front of the judge to urge him to pursue the date
